PT J
AU HARRIS, S
AF HARRIS, S
TI SPINAL ARTHRITIS (SPONDYLOSIS DEFORMANS) IN RED FOX, VULPES-VULPES, WITH
   SOME METHODOLOGY OF RELEVANCE TO ZOO-ARCHAEOLOGY
SO JOURNAL OF ARCHAEOLOGICAL SCIENCE
LA English
DT Article
AB The skeletons of 252 adult foxes killed in suburban London [England] were used to study the development of spondylosis deformans, a condition of the spinal column previously unrecorded in the red fox. Although the average age of the specimens was only 1 yr, 9 mo., 34.5% of the population were affected with spondylosis. The distribution of osteophytes on the vertebral column is shown, and factors such as age and trauma, which affect the development of the condition, are examined. The significance of such well-developed pathological conditions in a wild mammalian population is discussed.
